###########################
# Annexation Events
###########################
# By lots of folks
# Converted from on_actions to decisions by Rylock and Dr_Njitram
# Any new post-annexation events need to have their triggers in the KR_on_actions file
###########################

add_namespace = annex

country_event = { #Check for possible annexations
	id = annex.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.1" }

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { tag = XXA }
	}

	option = {
		# check Illyrian split exception
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = AUS
				HUN = { is_subject_of = AUS }
				109 = { is_owned_and_controlled_by = HUN }
			}
			109 = { check_potential_annexations = yes }
			every_owned_state = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
						is_controlled_by = ROOT
						is_in_array = { global.annexation_relevant_states = THIS }
					}
					check_potential_annexations = yes
				}
			}
		}
		# otherwise do regular check
		else = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_in_array = { global.annexation_relevant_states = THIS }
					is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
					is_controlled_by = ROOT
				}
				check_potential_annexations = yes
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = KR_checking_for_possible_annexations
	}
}

country_event = { #Swiss liberation
	id = annex.2
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.2" }
	title = annexation_SWI_CONQ
	desc = annexation_SWI_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.2.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				760 = {
					NOT = { is_core_of = SWI }
				}
			}
			760 = { add_core_of = SWI }
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = SWI
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			SWI = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 943
				is_french_tag = no
				NOT = {
					owns_state = 16
					owns_state = 21
					943 = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes }
					any_allied_country = {
						943 = { is_claim_or_core_of_PREV = yes }
					}
				}
			}
			SWI = { transfer_state = 943 }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = SWI }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
		if = {
			limit = { tag = GER }
			SWI = { complete_national_focus = SWI_german_aid }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = AUS }
			SWI = { complete_national_focus = SWI_austrian_assisstance }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_socialist_government = yes }
			SWI = {
				complete_national_focus = SWI_bend_to_france
				unlock_national_focus = SWI_referendum_syndicalism
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Take Romandie
		name = annex.2.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		trigger = {
			is_french_tag = yes
			owns_state = 760
		}
		add_state_claim = 760
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = SWI }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		SWI = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_socialist_government = yes }
				complete_national_focus = SWI_bend_to_france
				unlock_national_focus = SWI_referendum_syndicalism
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = SWI_CONQ
		occupy_medium_country = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Annexation of Bulgaria
	id = annex.3
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.3" }
	title = annexation_BUL_CONQ
	desc = annexation_BUL_CONQ_desc
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_temp_array = { core_removal_array = BUL }
			remove_all_cores_and_claims_of_tags = yes
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 48 #Sofia
						state = 211 #Burgas
						state = 212 #Plovdiv
						state = 770 #Pleven
						state = 771 #Varna
						state = 1090 #Vidin
					}
				}
				add_core_of = BUL
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.3.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = BUL }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			BUL = {
				add_state_claim = 77 #Silistria
				add_state_claim = 184 #Western Thrace
				add_state_claim = 769 #Eastern Salonica
				add_state_core = 1089 #Kardzhali
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = SER
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			# Pact members asked to give up land
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						tag = SER
						tag = BUL
					}
					is_in_faction_with = SER
				}
				country_event = pact.68
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #integrate
		name = eurasian_integration.option
		trigger = {
			tag = RUS
			OR = {
				has_government = totalist
				has_cosmetic_tag = RUS_EUR_bolshevist
				has_cosmetic_tag = RUS_EUR_national_maximalist
				AND = {
					has_cosmetic_tag = RUS_EUR
					has_government = national_populist
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = BUL
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_resistance = yes }
					set_temp_variable = { original_compliance = THIS.compliance }
					set_temp_variable = { original_resistance = THIS.resistance }
					cancel_resistance = yes
				}
				start_resistance = BUL
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_compliance }
					set_compliance = original_compliance
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_resistance }
					set_resistance = original_resistance
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no }
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -25
		add_to_array = { RUS_integration_array = BUL }
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}
	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			BUL = {
				add_state_core = 1089 #Kardzhali
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = BUL_CONQ
		occupy_medium_country = yes
	}
}

	title = annexation_ROM_CONQ
	desc = annexation_ROM_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {

				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 46 #Muntenia

				}

	}

	option = { #liberate

			factor = 40

				factor = 0

		}

				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
			}
		}
		add_state_claim = 78
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = ROM }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		var:tag_to_release = { setup_romanian_puppet_leaders = yes }
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = { RUS_russian_monarch = yes }
			}
			ROM = { 
				RUS_install_puppet_monarchy = yes
			}
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			76 = { add_claim_by = ROM } #North Transylvania
			1112 = { add_claim_by = ROM } #North Transylvania
			1117 = { add_claim_by = ROM } #North Transylvania
			1118 = { add_claim_by = ROM } #North Transylvania
			77 = { add_core_of = ROM } #Silistria

country_event = { #Serbian liberation
	id = annex.8
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.8" }
	title = annexation_SER_CONQ
	desc = annexation_SER_CONQ_desc

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_temp_array = { core_removal_array = SER }
			remove_all_cores_and_claims_of_tags = yes
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 107 #Belgrade
						state = 108 #Morava
						state = 767 #Nis
					}
				}
				add_core_of = SER
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.8.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = SER }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			765 = { add_core_of = SER }
		}
	}
	option = { #integrate
		name = eurasian_integration.option
		trigger = {
			tag = RUS
			OR = {
				has_government = totalist
				has_cosmetic_tag = RUS_EUR_bolshevist
				has_cosmetic_tag = RUS_EUR_national_maximalist
				AND = {
					has_cosmetic_tag = RUS_EUR
					has_government = national_populist
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = SER
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_resistance = yes }
					set_temp_variable = { original_compliance = THIS.compliance }
					set_temp_variable = { original_resistance = THIS.resistance }
					cancel_resistance = yes
				}
				start_resistance = SER
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_compliance }
					set_compliance = original_compliance
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_resistance }
					set_resistance = original_resistance
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no }
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -25
		add_to_array = { RUS_integration_array = SER }
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}
	option = { #make Yugoslavia
		trigger = {
			109 = {
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
			}
			104 = {
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
			}
			105 = {
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
			}
			NOT = {
				is_south_slav_tag = yes
				tag = AUS
				tag = HUN
			}
		}

		name = annex.8.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
				OR = {
					state = 102 #Carniola
					state = 1101 #Carniola
					state = 1103 #Carniola
					state = 1104 #Carniola
					state = 109 #Posavina
					state = 1102 #Posavina
					state = 103 #Lika
					state = 1099 #Lika
					state = 1105 #Lika
					state = 163 #Dalmatia
					state = 1098 #Dalmatia
					state = 104 #Bosnia
					state = 1141 #Bosnia
					state = 1142 #Bosnia
					state = 1143 #Bosnia
					state = 1145 #Bosnia
					state = 794 #Syrmia
					state = 1128 #Syrmia
					state = 767 #Nis
					state = 765 #Kosovo
					state = 105 #Montenegro
					state = 1097 #Montenegro
					state = 106 #Macedonia
					state = 841 #Pirot
					state = 736 #Austrian Littoral
					state = 1100 #Austrian Littoral
					state = 1144 #Austrian Littoral
					state = 45 #Vojvodina
					state = 875 #West Banat
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_claimed_by = SER }
				remove_claim_by = SER
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = SER } }
				add_core_of = SER
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = SER }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		SER = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = SER_YUG
		}
	}
	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = SER_CONQ
		occupy_medium_country = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Greece liberation
	id = annex.10
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.10" }
	title = annexation_GRE_CONQ
	desc = annexation_GRE_CONQ_desc

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_temp_array = { core_removal_array = GRE }
			remove_all_cores_and_claims_of_tags = yes
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 47 #Central Greece
						state = 182 #Crete
						state = 185 #Epirus
						state = 186 #Peloponnese
						state = 758 #Ionian Islands
						state = 768 #Thessaly
						state = 939 #Cyclades
						state = 1076 #Veria
					}
				}
				add_core_of = GRE
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Liberate Greece as republic
		name = annex.10.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					tag = GER
					tag = AUS
					is_in_faction_with = CAN
					is_in_faction_with = GBR
					AND = {
						has_government = authoritarian_democrat
						is_in_europe = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			has_socialist_government = no
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = GRE }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		GRE = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_socialist_government = yes }
				GRE_stop_being_syndicalist = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_cosmetic_tag = GRE_kingdom }
				GRE_restore_republic = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = GRE_monarchists_win_referendum }
				clr_country_flag = GRE_monarchists_win_referendum
				set_country_flag = GRE_republicans_win_referendum
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_government = authoritarian_democrat }
				add_popularity = { ideology = paternal_autocrat popularity = 0.20 }
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
					elections_allowed = no
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				add_state_core = 164 #Dodecanese
				add_state_core = 183 #Cyprus
				add_state_core = 187 #Aegean Islands
				add_state_core = 731 #Western Salonica
				add_state_claim = 769 #Eastern Salonica
				add_state_core = 989 #Chalcidice
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Liberate Kingdom of Greece
		name = annex.10.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				NOT = {
					tag = GER
					tag = AUS
					is_in_faction_with = CAN
					is_in_faction_with = GBR
					AND = {
						has_government = authoritarian_democrat
						is_in_europe = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			has_socialist_government = no
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = GRE }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		GRE = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_socialist_government = yes }
				GRE_stop_being_syndicalist = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = GRE_memories_of_king }
				remove_ideas = GRE_memories_of_king
			}
			if = {
				limit = { 	NOT = { has_cosmetic_tag = GRE_kingdom } }
				set_cosmetic_tag = GRE_kingdom
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = GRE_king_alexandros }
				hidden_effect = {
					country_event = gre.25
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = GRE_king_georgios }
				hidden_effect = {
					country_event = gre.26
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_completed_focus = GRE_restore_monarchy }
				hidden_effect = {
					country_event = gre.27
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { has_completed_focus = GRE_monarchy_referendum }
					ROOT = { has_elected_government = yes }
				}
				set_country_flag = GRE_monarchists_win_referendum
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = GRE_monarchy_referendum
					has_country_flag = GRE_republicans_win_referendum
				}
				set_country_flag = GRE_monarchists_win_referendum
				clr_country_flag = GRE_republicans_win_referendum
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT = { has_dictatorship_government = yes }
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					country_event = gre.27
				}
			}
			else = {
				hidden_effect = {
					country_event = gre.25
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				add_state_core = 164 #Dodecanese
				add_state_core = 183 #Cyprus
				add_state_core = 187 #Aegean Islands

							state = 1144
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { is_claimed_by = PREV }
						remove_claim_by = PREV
					}
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = PREV } }
						add_core_of = PREV
					}
					PREV = { transfer_state = PREV }
				}
				country_event = annex.18
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #annex
		name = annex.17.h
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = AUS
				tag = SER
				tag = CRO
				tag = ITA
				tag = SIC
				tag = SRI
				tag = SRD
				tag = VNC
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1000
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				736 = {
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
				OR = {
					tag = SER
					tag = ITA
					tag = SIC
					tag = SRI
					tag = SRD
					tag = VNC
				}
			}
			736 = { add_claim_by = ROOT }
			1100 = { add_claim_by = ROOT }
			1144 = { add_claim_by = ROOT }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = AUS
					tag = CRO
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 736
						state = 1100
						state = 1144
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_claimed_by = ROOT }
					remove_claim_by = ROOT
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT } }
					add_core_of = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = AUS
				tag = SER
				tag = CRO
				tag = ITA
				tag = SIC
				tag = SRI
				tag = SRD
				tag = VNC
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = AUS_LIT_CONQ
		occupy_small_country = yes
	}

				if = {

					set_temp_variable = { original_resistance = THIS.resistance }
					cancel_resistance = yes
				}
				start_resistance = CRO
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_compliance }
					set_compliance = original_compliance
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_resistance }
					set_resistance = original_resistance
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no }
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -25
		add_to_array = { RUS_integration_array = CRO }

			factor = 30
		}

			if = {

					NOT = { is_claimed_by = SER }
				}

			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					SER = { has_country_flag = SER_has_integrated_macedonia}
					is_claimed_by = SER
				}
				remove_claim_by = SER
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					SER = { has_country_flag = SER_has_integrated_macedonia}

				}

			}
			SER = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}

			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 230
				NOT = { country_exists = ARM }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = ARM }
			release_targeted_tag = yes
			if = {
				limit = { is_faction_leader = yes }
				add_to_faction = ARM
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 589
				NOT = { country_exists = ALO }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = ALO }
			release_targeted_tag = yes
			if = {
				limit = { is_faction_leader = yes }
				add_to_faction = ALO
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 405
				NOT = { country_exists = TRK }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = TRK }
			release_targeted_tag = yes
			if = {
				limit = { is_faction_leader = yes }
				add_to_faction = TRK
			}
		}

		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_siberia = yes
					AND = {
						is_owned_by = ROOT
						OR = {
							state = 582 #Orsk
							state = 573 #Zlatoust
							state = 581 #Northern Urals
						}
					}
				}
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				NOT = { is_core_of = SIB }
			}
			add_core_of = SIB
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = SIB }
		release_targeted_tag = yes

		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = ROOT
				NOT = {
					tag = ROOT
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_claim_or_core_or_ambition_of_PREV = yes
					OR = {
						is_core_of = RUS
						is_core_of = SOV
					}
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
				PREV = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = RUS
					is_core_of = SOV
				}
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}

			RUS = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = RUS }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.48.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		occupy_massive_country = yes
		set_country_flag = RUS_CONQ
	}
}

			has_socialist_government = yes
			owns_state = 13
			owns_state = 96
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
		}

			limit = {
				region = 37 #Baltic States

			}

				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = BAT }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
		setup_puppet_baltic_union = yes
	}

	option = { #restore UBD
		name = annex.61.b
		trigger = {
			tag = GER
			NOT = { country_exists = BAT }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
		}
		BAT = {
			add_state_core = 12 #Livonia
			add_state_core = 13 #Estonia
			add_state_core = 190 #Courland
			add_state_core = 191 #Northern Livonia
			add_state_core = 1091 #Riga
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = BAT }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
	}

	option = { #give to UBD
		name = annex.61.c
		trigger = {
			is_ally_with = BAT
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = BAT }
		add_to_temp_array = { target_cores_to_release = LAT }
		transfer_territory_from_core_regions = yes
	}

	option = { #Integrate
		name = annex.61.d
		trigger = {
			is_russian_tag = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				region = 37 #Baltic States
				is_core_of = LAT
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_resistance = yes }
					set_temp_variable = { original_compliance = THIS.compliance }
					set_temp_variable = { original_resistance = THIS.resistance }
					cancel_resistance = yes
				}
				start_resistance = LAT
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_compliance }
					set_compliance = original_compliance
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_resistance }
					set_resistance = original_resistance
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no }
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -25
		add_to_array = { RUS_integration_array = LAT }
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
			is_russian_tag = no
		}
		occupy_small_country = yes
		set_country_flag = LAT_CONQ
	}
}

	desc = annexation_SPA_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #give to carlists
		name = annex.66.a
		trigger = {
			has_socialist_government = no
			OR = {
				is_in_faction_with = CAR
				NOT = { country_exists = CAR }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 95
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = CAR
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
					OR = {
						is_core_of = SPR
						is_core_of = CAR
						is_core_of = CNT
					}
				}
				CAR = {
					add_state_core = PREV
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
					OR = {
						is_core_of = SPR
						is_core_of = CAR
						is_core_of = CNT
					}
				}
				CAR = {
					add_state_core = PREV
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = CAR }
			puppet_released_tag = yes
			CAR = {
				set_cosmetic_tag = CAR_kingdom
				set_country_flag = released_after_annexation
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #give to kingdom
		name = annex.66.b
		trigger = {
			has_socialist_government = no
			OR = {
				is_in_faction_with = SPR
				NOT = { country_exists = SPR }
			}
		}

			factor = 95
		}

				limit = {

					}

country_event = { #Irish Government
	id = annex.69
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.69" }
	title = annex.69
	desc = annex.69
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = annex.69.a
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_government = totalist
					has_government = syndicalist
					has_government = radical_socialist
				}
			}
			create_syndicalist_irish_government = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_government = social_conservative
					has_government = market_liberal
					has_government = social_liberal
					has_government = social_democrat
				}
			}
			create_democratic_irish_government = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_government = authoritarian_democrat
					has_government = paternal_autocrat
					has_government = national_populist
				}
			}
			create_autocratic_irish_government = yes
		}
	}
}

		}

				has_completed_focus = RUS_Expansionism
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = GEO }
		release_targeted_tag = yes

			}
			else = {

						popularity = 0.4
					}
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
						elections_allowed = no
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #republic
		name = annex.72.c
		trigger = {
			has_authoritarian_government = no
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_completed_focus = RUS_Expansionism
			}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = GEO }
		release_targeted_tag = yes

	option = { #Integrate
		name = annex.72.d
		trigger = {
			is_russian_tag = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				region = 134 #Caucasus
				is_core_of = GEO
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			add_claim_by = ROOT
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_resistance = yes }
					set_temp_variable = { original_compliance = THIS.compliance }
					set_temp_variable = { original_resistance = THIS.resistance }
					cancel_resistance = yes
				}
				start_resistance = GEO
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_compliance }
					set_compliance = original_compliance
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_resistance }
					set_resistance = original_resistance
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no }
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -25
		add_to_array = { RUS_integration_array = GEO }
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #Give to Russia
		name = annex.72.e
		trigger = {
			is_german_tag = no
			is_russian_tag = no
			any_allied_country = {
				is_russian_tag = yes

					is_russian_tag = yes
					is_ally_with = ROOT
				}
				set_temp_variable = { ROOT.tag_to_release = THIS }
			}
		}
		transfer_territory_from_core_regions = yes
	}

	option = { #occupation
		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = GEO_CONQ
		occupy_medium_country = yes
	}
}

						TRK_agrarian_socialism_1        
						TRK_fraternization 
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Split Turkestan
		name = annex.79.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_russian_tag = yes
			}
		}
		
		#Uzbekistan
		hidden_effect = {
			861 = { #Nukus
				add_core_of = UZB
				remove_core_of = TRK
			}
			584 = { #Nukus
				add_core_of = UZB
				remove_core_of = TRK
			}
		}
		
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = UZB }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		
		#Kokand
		hidden_effect = {
			586 = { #Pishpek
				add_core_of = KYR
				remove_core_of = ALO
			}
			1042 = { #Osh
				add_core_of = KYR
				remove_core_of = TRK
			}
			407 = { #Tashkent
				add_core_of = KYR
				remove_core_of = TRK
			}
			712 = { #Tashkent
				add_core_of = KYR
				remove_core_of = TRK
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = KYR }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		KYR = { set_cosmetic_tag = KYR_KOK }
		
		#Turkestan
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = TRK }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
	}
	option = { #Integrate
		name = annex.79.c
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = ALO
				tag = UZB
				tag = KYR
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = TRK
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
			}
			add_core_of = ROOT
		}
	}
	option = { #Integrate
		name = annex.79.c
		trigger = {
			is_russian_tag = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_in_array = { RUS.RUS_turkestan_region = THIS }
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			add_claim_by = ROOT
			remove_claim_by = UZB
			remove_claim_by = KYR
			remove_core_of = UZB
			remove_core_of = KYR
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_resistance = yes }
					set_temp_variable = { original_compliance = THIS.compliance }
					set_temp_variable = { original_resistance = THIS.resistance }
					cancel_resistance = yes
				}
				start_resistance = TRK
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_compliance }
					set_compliance = original_compliance
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_resistance }
					set_resistance = original_resistance
				}
			}
			
		}
		add_political_power = -40
		add_to_array = { RUS_integration_array = TRK }
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}
	option = { #give to Russian ally
		name = annex.80.e
		trigger = {
			any_allied_country = {
				is_russian_tag = yes
				owns_state = 219
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 80 }
		add_to_temp_array = { target_cores_to_release = TRK }
		hidden_effect = {
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_russian_tag = yes
					is_ally_with = ROOT
				}
				set_temp_variable = { ROOT.tag_to_release = THIS }
			}
		}
		transfer_territory_from_core_regions = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
			is_russian_tag = no
		}
		set_country_flag = TRK_CONQ
		occupy_large_country = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			for_each_scope_loop = {
				array = RUS.RUS_turkestan_region
				add_core_of = TRK
			}
		}
	}
}

				start_resistance = ALO
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_compliance }
					set_compliance = original_compliance
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_resistance }
					set_resistance = original_resistance
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no }
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -10
		add_to_array = { RUS_integration_array = ALO }
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #give to Russian ally
		name = annex.80.e
		trigger = {
			is_russian_tag = no
			any_allied_country = {
				is_russian_tag = yes
				owns_state = 219
			}
		}
		ai_chance = { base = 80 }
		add_to_temp_array = { target_cores_to_release = ALO }
		hidden_effect = {
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_russian_tag = yes
					is_ally_with = ROOT
				}
				set_temp_variable = { ROOT.tag_to_release = THIS }
			}
		}
		transfer_territory_from_core_regions = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
			is_russian_tag = no
		}
		set_country_flag = ALO_CONQ
		occupy_large_country = yes
	}
}

		}

			factor = 0
		}

		add_state_claim = 151

country_event = { #The Annexation of Arabia
	id = annex.106
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.106" }
	title = annexation_ARA_CONQ
	desc = annexation_ARA_CONQ_desc

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_temp_array = { core_removal_array = JBS }
			add_to_temp_array = { core_removal_array = SAU }
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { country_exists = HEJ }
				}
				add_to_temp_array = { core_removal_array = HEJ }
				remove_all_cores_and_claims_of_tags = yes
				679 = { add_core_of = HEJ } #Hejaz
				754 = { add_core_of = HEJ } #Medina
			}
			else = {
				remove_all_cores_and_claims_of_tags = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #release Arabia
		name = annex.106.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { country_exists = HEJ }
				OR = {
					679 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes } #Hejaz
					754 = { is_valid_annexation_state = yes } #Medina
				}
			}
			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = HEJ }
		}
		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = JBS }
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_arabia = yes
					AND = {
						OR = {
							state = 679 #Hejaz
							state = 754 #Medina
						}
						check_variable = { tag_to_release = HEJ }
					}
				}
			}
			add_core_of = var:tag_to_release
		}
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		var:tag_to_release = {
			if = {
				limit = { tag = HEJ }
				set_cosmetic_tag = HEJ_ARA
			}
		}

		### Apply League of Arab States modifiers if SYR/IRQ
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = IRQ
				has_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = IRQ_League_of_Arab_States_dynamic_modifier
					scope = IRQ
				}
			}
			var:tag_to_release = {
				add_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = IRQ_League_of_Arab_States_dynamic_modifier
					scope = IRQ
				}
				set_country_flag = joined_loa
			}	
			IRQ = {
				add_to_variable = {
					var = var_LOA_members
					value = 0.01
				}
				country_event = irqfor.5
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = SYR
				has_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = IRQ_League_of_Arab_States_dynamic_modifier
					scope = SYR
				}
			}
			var:tag_to_release = {
				add_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = SYR_League_of_Arab_States_dynamic_modifier
					scope = SYR
				}
				set_country_flag = joined_loa
			}			
			SYR = {
				add_to_variable = {
					var = var_LOA_members
					value = 0.01
				}
				country_event = syrfor.2
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Give to HEJ
		name = annex.106.b
		trigger = {
			is_ally_with = HEJ
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = HEJ }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = { is_arabia = yes }
			transfer_state_and_add_core = yes
		}
		var:tag_to_release = { set_cosmetic_tag = HEJ_ARA }
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = { is_ai = no }
		occupy_medium_country = yes
		set_country_flag = ARA_CONQ
	}
}

country_event = { #The Annexation of Persia

	id = annex.109
	title = annexation_PER_CONQ
	desc = annexation_PER_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { tag = OTT }
				add_state_claim = 347 #Khasab
				add_state_claim = 413 #Khuzestan
				add_state_claim = 417 #Western Azerbaijan
				add_state_claim = 419 #Eastern Azerbaijan
				add_state_claim = 421 #Kurdistan
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { tag = IRQ }
				add_state_claim = 413 #Khuzestan
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #puppet
		name = annex.109.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 99
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = PER
					AND = {
						is_claimed_by = PER
						is_clear_other_claims = yes
					}
					AND = {
						state = 352 #Van
						ROOT = {
							NOT = {
								owns_state = 291 #Baghdad
								owns_state = 49 #Ankara
							}
						}
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
					region = 28 #Syria
					region = 129 #Anatolia
					region = 239 #Mesopotamia
					AND = {
						OR = {
							state = 418 #Golestan
							state = 420 #Mazandaran
							state = 804 #Northern Khorasan
						}
						ROOT = { is_russian_tag = yes }
					}
				}
			}

			PER = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = PER }
		puppet_released_tag = yes

		hidden_effect = {
			var:tag_to_release = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_socialist_government = no }
					remove_ideas = {
						PER_beacon_mideast_socialism
						PER_evolution_idea
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_elected_government = no }
					remove_ideas = PER_shining_democracy
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_authoritarian_government = no }
					remove_ideas = PER_legacy_of_agha_khan
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = { RUS_russian_monarch = yes }
					}
					PER = { 
						RUS_install_puppet_monarchy = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #integrate
		name = eurasian_integration.option
		trigger = {
			tag = RUS
			OR = {
				has_government = totalist
				has_cosmetic_tag = RUS_EUR_bolshevist
				has_cosmetic_tag = RUS_EUR_national_maximalist
				has_cosmetic_tag = RUS_EUR
				has_cosmetic_tag = RUS_EUR_empire
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = PER
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_resistance = yes }
					set_temp_variable = { original_compliance = THIS.compliance }
					set_temp_variable = { original_resistance = THIS.resistance }
					cancel_resistance = yes
				}
				start_resistance = PER
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_compliance }
					set_compliance = original_compliance
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_resistance }
					set_resistance = original_resistance
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no }
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -25
		add_to_array = { RUS_integration_array = PER }
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}
	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = { is_ai = no }
		occupy_medium_country = yes
		set_country_flag = PER_CONQ
	}
}

		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = SYR
				has_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = IRQ_League_of_Arab_States_dynamic_modifier
					scope = SYR
				}
			}
			var:tag_to_release = {
				add_dynamic_modifier = {
					modifier = SYR_League_of_Arab_States_dynamic_modifier
					scope = SYR
				}
				set_country_flag = joined_loa
			}			
			SYR = {
				add_to_variable = {
					var = var_LOA_members
					value = 0.01
				}
				country_event = syrfor.2
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = { is_ai = no }
		occupy_medium_country = yes
		set_country_flag = YEM_CONQ
	}
}

country_event = { #The Annexation of Armenia
	id = annex.113
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.113" }
	title = annexation_ARM_CONQ
	desc = annexation_ARM_CONQ_desc

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #puppet
		name = annex.113.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				add = 0
				tag = PER
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_completed_focus = RUS_Expansionism
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = ARM }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = var:tag_to_release
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
				if = {
					limit = { state = 998 } #Highland Karabakh
					990 = { is_valid_annexation_state = no } #Baku
					AZE = { ROOT_can_grant_land = no }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { state = 1082 } #Lori
					231 = { is_valid_annexation_state = no } #Sakartvelo
					GEO = { ROOT_can_grant_land = no }
				}
			}
			var:tag_to_release = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		puppet_released_tag = yes
	}

	option = { #Integrate
		name = annex.113.b
		trigger = {
			is_russian_tag = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				region = 134 #Caucasus
				is_core_of = ARM
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			add_claim_by = ROOT
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_resistance = yes }
					set_temp_variable = { original_compliance = THIS.compliance }
					set_temp_variable = { original_resistance = THIS.resistance }
					cancel_resistance = yes
				}
				start_resistance = ARM
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_compliance }
					set_compliance = original_compliance
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_resistance }
					set_resistance = original_resistance
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no }
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -20
		add_to_array = { RUS_integration_array = ARM }
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #Integrate
		name = annex.17.h
		trigger = {
			tag = PER
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1000
		}
		occupy_small_country = yes
		set_country_flag = ARM_CONQ
		add_state_claim = 230
		add_state_claim = 998
	}

	option = { #Give to Russia
		name = annex.113.c
		trigger = {
			is_german_tag = no
			is_russian_tag = no
			any_allied_country = {
				is_russian_tag = yes
				owns_state = 219
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				add = 0
				tag = PER
			}
		}
		add_to_temp_array = { target_cores_to_release = ARM }
		hidden_effect = {
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_russian_tag = yes
					is_ally_with = ROOT
				}
				set_temp_variable = { ROOT.tag_to_release = THIS }
			}
		}
		transfer_territory_from_core_regions = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = {
			is_russian_tag = no
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 1000
				tag = PER
			}
		}
		occupy_small_country = yes
		set_country_flag = ARM_CONQ
	}
}

country_event = { #The Annexation of the Ukraine
	id = annex.123
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.123" }

	desc = annexation_UKR_CONQ_desc

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		UKR_remove_king = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { tag = RUS }
					check_variable = { RUS.UKR_original_generals^num > 0 }
				}
				for_each_scope_loop = {
					array = RUS.UKR_original_generals
					set_nationality = UKR
				}
				clear_array = RUS.UKR_original_generals
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Puppet
		name = annex.123.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_russian_tag = yes
			}
		}

		release_targeted_tag_with_claims = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			UKR = { set_cosmetic_tag = UKR_republican }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = { RUS_russian_monarch = yes }
			}
			UKR = { 
				RUS_install_puppet_monarchy = yes
			}

		}

		}

		}

			is_russian_tag = yes
		}

			base = 100
		}

				OR = {
					region = 130 #Western Ukraine

			}
			add_claim_by = ROOT
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_resistance = yes }
					set_temp_variable = { original_compliance = THIS.compliance }
					set_temp_variable = { original_resistance = THIS.resistance }
					cancel_resistance = yes
				}
				start_resistance = UKR
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_compliance }
					set_compliance = original_compliance
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_resistance }
					set_resistance = original_resistance
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no }
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -100
		add_to_array = { RUS_integration_array = UKR }
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #Give to Russia
		name = annex.123.d
		trigger = {
			is_german_tag = no
			is_russian_tag = no

				is_russian_tag = yes
				owns_state = 219
			}

		}

	}

			is_russian_tag = no

	}

	desc = annexation_CAF_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = annex.140.a #Liberate the West Indies Federation
		trigger = {
			NOT = { tag = CAN }
			count_triggers = {
				amount = 3
				309 = { #Suriname
					is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
					is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
				}
				686 = { #Puerto Rico
					is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
					is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
				}
				687 = { #Guyana
					is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
					is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
				}

					is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
					is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
				}
				691 = { #Trinidad
					is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
					is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_caribbean_fed = yes
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
				if = {

					remove_claim_by = CAF
				}
				add_core_of = CAF
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_caribbean_fed = yes
					OR = {
						NOT = { is_owned_by = ROOT }
						is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_core_of = CAF }
					remove_core_of = CAF
					add_claim_by = CAF
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { tag = HOL }
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							state = 695 #Curacao
							state = 1038 #Suriname Jungle
							state = 1077 #Saint Martin
							state = 309 #Suriname
						}
					}
					remove_core_of = CAF
					remove_claim_by = CAF
				}
			}
		}
		
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = CAF }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_socialist_government = yes }
			var:tag_to_release = { complete_national_focus = CAF_syndicalist_revolution }
		}
		else = {
			var:tag_to_release = { clr_country_flag = CAF_syndie_revolution }
		}
	}
	option = { #Canada option 1, puppeting them back
		name = annex.140.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		trigger = {
			tag = CAN
			count_triggers = {
				amount = 3
				309 = { #Suriname
					is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
					is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
				}
				686 = { #Puerto Rico
					is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
					is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
				}
				687 = { #Guyana
					is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
					is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
				}
				689 = { #Jamaica
					is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
					is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
				}
				691 = { #Trinidad
					is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
					is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_caribbean_fed = yes
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_claimed_by = CAF }
					remove_claim_by = CAF
				}
				add_core_of = CAF
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_caribbean_fed = yes
					OR = {
						NOT = { is_owned_by = ROOT }
						is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_core_of = CAF }
					remove_core_of = CAF
					add_claim_by = CAF
				}
			}
		}

					state = 91
					state = 1140
					state = 89
					state = 1126
					state = 1127
				}
			}
			remove_core_of = GAL
			if = {
				limit = { is_claimed_by = UKR }
				remove_claim_by = UKR
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = UKR } }
				add_core_of = UKR
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #annex
		name = annex.17.h
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = POL
				tag = UKR
				AND = {
					tag = AUS
					AUS_is_unified = yes
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1000

				tag = UKR

			}
		}

					set_temp_variable = { original_resistance = THIS.resistance }
					cancel_resistance = yes
				}

					limit = { has_variable = original_compliance }

			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_claimed_by = CRO }
				remove_claim_by = CRO
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = CRO } }
				add_core_of = CRO
			}

		}

		}

			NOT = {

			}

		}
	}
	option = { #integrate
		name = eurasian_integration.option
		trigger = {
			tag = RUS
			OR = {
				has_government = totalist
				has_cosmetic_tag = RUS_EUR_bolshevist
				has_cosmetic_tag = RUS_EUR_national_maximalist
				AND = {
					has_cosmetic_tag = RUS_EUR
					has_government = national_populist
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = BOS
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_resistance = yes }
					set_temp_variable = { original_compliance = THIS.compliance }
					set_temp_variable = { original_resistance = THIS.resistance }
					cancel_resistance = yes
				}
				start_resistance = BOS
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_compliance }
					set_compliance = original_compliance
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_resistance }
					set_resistance = original_resistance
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no }
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -25
		add_to_array = { RUS_integration_array = BOS }
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

			OR = {
				tag = CRO
				tag = SER
				AND = {
					tag = AUS
					AUS_is_unified = yes

			}

			factor = 1000
		}

			104 = { add_claim_by = ROOT }
		}

						state = 1145

				}

			}
		}

		}

			limit = {
				region = 37 #Baltic States
				is_core_of = LIT
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
			}
			add_claim_by = ROOT
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_resistance = yes }
					set_temp_variable = { original_compliance = THIS.compliance }
					set_temp_variable = { original_resistance = THIS.resistance }
					cancel_resistance = yes
				}
				start_resistance = LIT
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_compliance }
					set_compliance = original_compliance
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_resistance }
					set_resistance = original_resistance
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no }
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -40
		add_to_array = { RUS_integration_array = LIT }
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
			is_russian_tag = no
		}
		set_country_flag = LIT_CONQ
		occupy_medium_country = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Fate of Mongolia
	id = annex.175
	title = annexation_MON_CONQ
	desc = annexation_MON_CONQ_desc

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.175"
		determine_chinese_ally = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { tag = RUS }
				add_state_claim = 329
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Release Mongolia
		name = annex.175.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 95
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				any_owned_state = {
					region = 222 #Inner Mongolia
				}
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				region = 152 #Outer Mongolia
			}
			MON = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = MON }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			var:tag_to_release = {
				load_focus_tree = {
					tree = mongolia_non_sternberg
					keep_completed = yes
				}
			}
		}
		setup_puppet_leader_MON = yes
	}
	option = { #Integrate
		name = annex.175.e
		trigger = {
			tag = RUS
			RUS = {
				OR = {
					has_idea = RUS_Nikolay_S_Trubetskoy_hog_sco
					has_idea = RUS_Lev_N_Gumilov_hog_pau
					has_idea = RUS_Georgiy_V_Vernadskiy_for_sli
					has_idea = RUS_Nikolay_S_Trubetskoy_for_sco
					has_idea = RUS_Lev_N_Gumilov_for_pau
					has_idea = RUS_Konstantin_A_Chkheidze_eco_ade
					has_idea = RUS_Pyetr_N_Savitskiy_sec_ade
					has_cosmetic_tag = RUS_EUR
					has_cosmetic_tag = RUS_EUR_national_maximalist
					has_cosmetic_tag = RUS_EUR_empire
					has_cosmetic_tag = RUS_EUR_bolshevist
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = MON
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			add_claim_by = ROOT
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_resistance = yes }
					set_temp_variable = { original_compliance = THIS.compliance }
					set_temp_variable = { original_resistance = THIS.resistance }
					cancel_resistance = yes
				}
				start_resistance = MON
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_compliance }
					set_compliance = original_compliance
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_resistance }
					set_resistance = original_resistance
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no }
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -25
		add_to_array = { RUS_integration_array = MON }
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}
	
	option = { #Release Greater Mongolia
		name = annex.175.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 95
		}
		trigger = {
			is_han_chinese_tag = no
			any_owned_state = {

			}
		}

					region = 152 #Outer Mongolia
					region = 222 #Inner Mongolia
				}
			}

				add_state_core = PREV
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = MON }

			var:tag_to_release = {

				}
			}
		}

country_event = { #Fate of Tibet
	id = annex.176
	title = annexation_TIB_CONQ
	desc = annexation_TIB_CONQ_desc

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.176"
		determine_chinese_ally = yes
	}

	option = { #Release Tibet
		name = annex.176.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 95
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				any_owned_state = {
					OR = {
						region = 220 #Xibei
						state = 601 #Xikang
					}
				}
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				region = 146 #Himalayas
				is_core_of = TIB
			}
			TIB = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = TIB }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
		setup_puppet_leader_TIB = yes
	}

	option = { #Release Greater Tibet
		name = annex.176.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 95
		}
		trigger = {
			is_han_chinese_tag = no
			any_owned_state = {
				OR = {
					region = 220 #Xibei
					state = 601 #Xikang
				}
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				OR = {
					region = 146 #Himalayas
					region = 220 #Xibei
					state = 601 #Xikang
				}
				OR = {
					is_core_of = TIB
					is_claimed_by = TIB
				}
			}
			TIB = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = TIB }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
	}

	option = { #Split between Tibet and China
		name = annex.176.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 95
		}
		trigger = {
			is_han_chinese_tag = no
			any_owned_state = {
				OR = {
					region = 220 #Xibei
					state = 601 #Xikang
					state = 693 #Chamdo
				}
			}
			has_event_target = china_ally_target
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				OR = {
					region = 220 #Xibei
					state = 601 #Xikang
					state = 693 #Chamdo
				}
			}
			event_target:china_ally_target = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				region = 146 #Himalayas
				is_core_of = TIB
			}
			TIB = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = TIB }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
	}

	option = { #Give it to China
		name = annex.174.m
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 95
		}
		trigger = {
			is_han_chinese_tag = no
			has_event_target = china_ally_target
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = event_target:china_ally_target modifier = KR_returned_land }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				OR = {
					region = 220 #Xibei
					state = 601 #Xikang
					is_core_of = TIB
				}
			}
			event_target:china_ally_target = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		occupy_medium_country = yes
		set_country_flag = TIB_CONQ
	}
}

country_event = { #Release Ma Clique (for Mongolia)
	id = annex.177
	title = annexation_XSM_CONQ
	desc = annexation_XSM_CONQ_desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_SIK_mongols

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.177"
		random_other_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = MON
					tag = TIB
				}
			}
			save_event_target_as = northwest_war_ally
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = annex.177.a
		#Transfer Tibetan/Mongolian States
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_event_target = northwest_war_ally
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 353
						state = 604
						state = 621
						state = 616
						state = 348
					}
					OR = {
						is_core_of = event_target:northwest_war_ally
						is_claimed_by = event_target:northwest_war_ally
					}
				}
				event_target:northwest_war_ally = {
					add_state_claim = PREV
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
		}

		#Release XSM
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = XSM
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			XSM = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		event_target:northwest_war_ally = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = XSM
					NOT = {
						is_core_of = event_target:northwest_war_ally
						is_claimed_by = event_target:northwest_war_ally
					}
				}
				XSM = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = XSM }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
		setup_puppet_leader_XSM = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		occupy_medium_country = yes
		set_country_flag = XSM_CONQ
	}
}

country_event = { #Fate of Manchuria
	id = annex.178
	title = annexation_MAN_CONQ
	desc = annexation_MAN_CONQ_desc

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.178"
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						tag = RUS
						tag = TRM
					}
				}
			}
			determine_chinese_ally = yes
		}
	}

	option = { #Release Independent Manchuria
		name = annex.178.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = { country_exists = MAN }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				add = 99
				tag = JAP
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_manchuria = yes
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			MAN = {
				add_state_core = PREV
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = JAP }
			hidden_effect = {
				set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = MAN }
				puppet_released_tag = yes
			}
			set_autonomy = {
				target = MAN
				autonomy_state = kr_special_autonomous_dependency
			}
			MAN = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = market_liberal
					elections_allowed = no
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = MAN }
			puppet_released_tag = yes
		}
	}

	option = { #Release the Left Kuomintang
		name = annex.174.a
		trigger = {
			has_socialist_government = yes
			NOT = { country_exists = CHI }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = CHI }
		release_chinese_government_in_manchuria = yes
		CHI = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = CHI_ROC
		}
	}

	option = { #Release the League of Eight Provinces
		name = annex.174.e
		trigger = {
			tag = GER
			NOT = { country_exists = LEP }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = LEP }
		release_chinese_government_in_manchuria = yes
		LEP = {
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = LEP_CHI
			hidden_effect = {
				set_potential_national_government = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Release the Left Kuomintang
		name = annex.174.f
		trigger = {
			is_russian_tag = yes
			has_global_flag = Russia_Supports_LKMT
			NOT = { country_exists = CHI }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = CHI }
		release_chinese_government_in_manchuria = yes
		CHI = {
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = social_democrat
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = CHI_ROC
		}
	}

	option = { #Release the Right Kuomintang
		name = annex.174.g
		trigger = {
			is_russian_tag = yes
			has_global_flag = Russia_Supports_RKMT
			NOT = { country_exists = GXC }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = GXC }
		release_chinese_government_in_manchuria = yes
		GXC = {
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = CHI_ROC
			load_focus_tree = KR_RKMT
			hidden_effect = {
				set_potential_national_government = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Release the Qing Empire
		name = annex.174.h
		trigger = {
			is_russian_tag = yes
			OR = {
				has_global_flag = Russia_Supports_QIE
				has_global_flag = Russia_Supports_ZHI
			}
			NOT = { country_exists = QIE }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = QIE }
		release_chinese_government_in_manchuria = yes
	}

	option = { #Release a Federalist China
		name = annex.174.i
		trigger = {
			has_elected_government = yes
			NOT = {
				tag = JAP
				tag = GER
				tag = RUS
				tag = TRM
				tag = LEC
			}
			NOT = { country_exists = GXC }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		GXC = {
			save_event_target_as = released_china_tag
		}
		release_chinese_government_in_manchuria = yes
		GXC = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = big_chen_mingshu
						has_country_flag = big_chen_lianbo
					}
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = social_liberal
					elections_allowed = no
				}
			}
			else = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = social_democrat
					elections_allowed = no
				}
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = UPC
			load_focus_tree = Federalist_China_Tree
			hidden_effect = {
				set_potential_national_government = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Release a Federalist China
		name = annex.174.i
		trigger = {
			is_russian_tag = yes
			has_global_flag = Russia_Supports_Federalists
			NOT = { country_exists = GXC }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		GXC = {
			save_event_target_as = released_china_tag
		}
		release_chinese_government_in_manchuria = yes
		GXC = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = big_chen_mingshu
						has_country_flag = big_chen_lianbo
					}
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = social_liberal
					elections_allowed = no
				}
			}
			else = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = social_democrat
					elections_allowed = no
				}
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = UPC
			load_focus_tree = Federalist_China_Tree
			hidden_effect = {
				set_potential_national_government = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Release the Beiyang Republic
		name = annex.174.j
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					NOT = {
						tag = JAP
						tag = GER
						tag = RUS
					}
					has_authoritarian_government = yes
				}
				tag = LEC
			}
			NOT = { country_exists = QIE }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = QIE }
		release_chinese_government_in_manchuria = yes
		QIE = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = QIE_ZHL
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Yan Huiqing"
				desc = "POLITICS_UPC_YAN_HUIQING_DESC"
				picture = "gfx/leaders/QIE/Portrait_QIE_Yan_Huiqing.png"
				expire = "1965.1.1"
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Release the Fengtian Government
		name = annex.174.b
		trigger = {
			tag = JAP
			FNG_JAP_hostile = no
			NOT = { country_exists = FNG }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = FNG }
		release_chinese_government_in_manchuria = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			set_autonomy = {
				target = FNG
				autonomy_state = kr_special_autonomous_dependency
			}
			FNG = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
					elections_allowed = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Release the Fengtian Government
		name = annex.174.b
		trigger = {
			tag = TRM
			has_global_flag = Russia_Supports_FNG
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		FNG = { save_event_target_as = released_china_tag }
		release_chinese_government_in_manchuria = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			FNG = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
					elections_allowed = no
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Take the coast, release FNG
		name = annex.174.c
		trigger = {
			tag = JAP
			FNG_JAP_hostile = no
			NOT = { country_exists = FNG }
			any_owned_state = {
				is_manchuria = yes
				has_variable = ambition_area_@ROOT
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_manchuria = yes
				is_china_claim_of_JAP = no
				NOT = { has_variable = ambition_area_@JAP }
			}
			FNG = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		set_autonomy = {
			target = FNG
			autonomy_state = kr_special_autonomous_dependency
		}
		FNG = {
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
				elections_allowed = no
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Give it to China
		name = annex.174.m
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 95
		}
		trigger = {
			is_han_chinese_tag = no
			has_event_target = china_ally_target
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = event_target:china_ally_target modifier = KR_returned_land }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				is_manchuria = yes
				if = {
					limit = { ROOT = { tag = JAP } }
					NOT = { has_variable = ambition_area_@ROOT }
				}
			}
			event_target:china_ally_target = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
	}
	option = { #Integrate
		name = annex.179.b 
		trigger = {
			tag = RUS
			RUS = {
				OR = {
					has_idea = RUS_Nikolay_S_Trubetskoy_hog_sco
					has_idea = RUS_Lev_N_Gumilov_hog_pau
					has_idea = RUS_Georgiy_V_Vernadskiy_for_sli
					has_idea = RUS_Nikolay_S_Trubetskoy_for_sco
					has_idea = RUS_Lev_N_Gumilov_for_pau
					has_idea = RUS_Konstantin_A_Chkheidze_eco_ade
					has_idea = RUS_Pyetr_N_Savitskiy_sec_ade
					has_cosmetic_tag = RUS_EUR
					has_cosmetic_tag = RUS_EUR_national_maximalist
					has_cosmetic_tag = RUS_EUR_empire
					has_cosmetic_tag = RUS_EUR_bolshevist
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_manchuria = yes
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			MAN = {
				add_state_core = PREV
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_manchuria = yes
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			remove_cores_of_dead_tags = yes
			add_claim_by = ROOT
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_resistance = yes }
					set_temp_variable = { original_compliance = THIS.compliance }
					set_temp_variable = { original_resistance = THIS.resistance }
					cancel_resistance = yes
				}
				start_resistance = MAN
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_compliance }
					set_compliance = original_compliance
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_resistance }
					set_resistance = original_resistance
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no }
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -25
		add_to_array = { RUS_integration_array = MAN }
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}
	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		occupy_large_country = yes
		set_country_flag = MAN_CONQ
	}
}

country_event = { #Fate of Xinjiang
	id = annex.179
	title = annexation_SIK_CONQ
	desc = annexation_SIK_CONQ_desc

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.179"
		determine_chinese_ally = yes
	}

	option = { #Release an independent Xinjiang
		name = annex.179.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 95
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				any_owned_state = {
					OR = {
						region = 220 #Xibei
						state = 601 #Xikang
					}
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = ETS }
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
					region = 221 #Xinjiang
				}
				ETS = {
					add_state_core = PREV
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
			puppet_released_tag = yes
			var:tag_to_release = { set_cosmetic_tag = ETS_puppet }
		}
	}

	option = { #Give it to China
		name = annex.174.m
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 95
		}
		trigger = {
			is_han_chinese_tag = no
			has_event_target = china_ally_target
		}
		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = event_target:china_ally_target modifier = KR_returned_land }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
				region = 221 #Xinjiang
			}
			event_target:china_ally_target = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
	}
	option = { #Integrate
		name = annex.179.b 
		trigger = {
			tag = RUS
			RUS = {
				OR = {
					has_idea = RUS_Nikolay_S_Trubetskoy_hog_sco
					has_idea = RUS_Lev_N_Gumilov_hog_pau
					has_idea = RUS_Georgiy_V_Vernadskiy_for_sli
					has_idea = RUS_Nikolay_S_Trubetskoy_for_sco
					has_idea = RUS_Lev_N_Gumilov_for_pau
					has_idea = RUS_Konstantin_A_Chkheidze_eco_ade
					has_idea = RUS_Pyetr_N_Savitskiy_sec_ade
					has_cosmetic_tag = RUS_EUR
					has_cosmetic_tag = RUS_EUR_national_maximalist
					has_cosmetic_tag = RUS_EUR_empire
					has_cosmetic_tag = RUS_EUR_bolshevist
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		remove_cores_of_dead_tags  = yes
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				region = 221
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}
			add_claim_by = ROOT
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_resistance = yes }
					set_temp_variable = { original_compliance = THIS.compliance }
					set_temp_variable = { original_resistance = THIS.resistance }
					cancel_resistance = yes
				}
				start_resistance = EST
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_compliance }
					set_compliance = original_compliance
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_resistance }
					set_resistance = original_resistance
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no }
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -25
		add_to_array = { RUS_integration_array = ETS }
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}
	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		occupy_medium_country = yes
		set_country_flag = SIK_CONQ
	}
}

country_event = { #Fate of the Legation Cities
	id = annex.180
	title = annexation_LEC_CONQ
	desc = annexation_LEC_CONQ_desc

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.180"
		determine_chinese_ally = yes
	}

	option = { #Release the Legation Cities
		name = annex.180.a
		trigger = {
			has_socialist_government = no
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_event_target = china_ally_target
				NOT = {
					tag = AUS
					tag = BEL
					tag = RUS
					tag = USA
					tag = CAL
					tag = TEX
					tag = GBR
					tag = GER
				}
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = LEC }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
				OR = {
					is_core_of = LEC
					is_possible_legation_cities_state = yes
				}
			}
			remove_claim_and_add_core_of_target = yes
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = var:tag_to_release
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
			}
			var:tag_to_release = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = GER
				}
				LEC = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
					}
					set_popularities = {
						totalist = 0
						radical_socialist = 0
						syndicalist = 0
						social_democrat = 2
						social_liberal = 10
						market_liberal = 8
						social_conservative = 3
						authoritarian_democrat = 12
						paternal_autocrat = 63
						national_populist = 2
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					tag = JAP
				}
				LEC = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = national_populist
					}
					set_popularities = {
						totalist = 0
						radical_socialist = 0
						syndicalist = 0
						social_democrat = 2
						social_liberal = 10
						market_liberal = 8
						social_conservative = 3
						authoritarian_democrat = 12
						paternal_autocrat = 3
						national_populist = 62
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						tag = AST
						tag = CAN
						tag = GBR
					}
				}
				LEC = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = social_conservative
					}
					set_popularities = {
						totalist = 0
						radical_socialist = 0
						syndicalist = 0
						social_democrat = 2
						social_liberal = 10
						market_liberal = 8
						social_conservative = 63
						authoritarian_democrat = 12
						paternal_autocrat = 3
						national_populist = 2
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				LEC = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = market_liberal
					}
					set_popularities = {
						totalist = 0
						radical_socialist = 0
						syndicalist = 0
						social_democrat = 2
						social_liberal = 23
						market_liberal = 28
						social_conservative = 13
						authoritarian_democrat = 12
						paternal_autocrat = 10
						national_populist = 2
					}
				}
			}
			ROOT = {
				country_event = lec.125
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						tag = USA
						tag = CAL
						tag = TEX
						tag = AUS
						tag = NEE
						tag = BEL
						tag = GER
						tag = GEX
						tag = CAN
						tag = GBR
						tag = JAP
						tag = RUS
						tag = TRM
					}
					exists = yes
					is_subject = no
					has_socialist_government = no
				}
				country_event = lec.125
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Give it to China

			factor = 80
		}

			is_han_chinese_tag = no

country_event = { #Fate of Brazil
	id = annex.181
	title = annexation_BRA_CONQ
	desc = annexation_BRA_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.181"
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { tag = PAR }
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
						OR = {
							state = 1041 #Iguassu
							state = 1043 #Ponta Pora
						}
					}
					add_claim_by = PAR
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { tag = ARG }
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							state = 502 #Rio Grande do Sul
							state = 1041 #Iguassu
							AND = {
								state = 1043 #Ponta Pora
								ARG = { owns_state = 301 } #Paraguay
							}
						}
					}
					add_claim_by = ARG
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #liberate full brazil
		name = annex.181.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = BRA
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = { has_country_flag = PIR_CONQ }
					}
					NOT = { region = 203 } #Uruguay Basin
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = { has_country_flag = SPO_CONQ }
					}
					NOT = { state = 501 } #SÃ£o Paulo
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = { has_country_flag = GOY_CONQ }
					}
					NOT = { region = 201 } #Central Brazil
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = { has_country_flag = BAH_CONQ }
					}
					NOT = { state = 499 } #Bahia
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = { has_country_flag = GRP_CONQ }
					}
					NOT = {
						state = 497 #Piaui
						state = 498 #Northeastern Brazil
						state = 896 #MaranhÃ£o
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = { has_country_flag = AMA_CONQ }
					}
					NOT = { region = 163 } #Amazonas
				}
			}
			BRA = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = BRA }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_government = national_populist }
				BRA = {
					complete_national_focus = BRA_AIB
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_government = paternal_autocrat }
				BRA = {
					complete_national_focus = BRA_new_state
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_government = radical_socialist
						AND = {
							has_government = social_democrat
							has_country_flag = soc_dems_are_socialists
						}
					}
				}
				BRA = {
					complete_national_focus = BRA_the_counter_coup
					complete_national_focus = BRA_f_anarchist_b
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_government = syndicalist }
				BRA = {
					complete_national_focus = BRA_the_counter_coup
					complete_national_focus = BRA_syndicalist_alliance
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_government = totalist }
				BRA = {
					complete_national_focus = BRA_the_counter_coup
					complete_national_focus = BRA_ato_institucional_1
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Balkanise Brazil
		name = annex.181.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				tag = ARG
			}
		}
		setup_brazilian_splinters = yes

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = PIR }
		release_targeted_tag_with_claims = yes

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = BAH }
		release_targeted_tag_with_claims = yes

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = SPO }
		release_targeted_tag_with_claims = yes

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = AMA }
		release_targeted_tag_with_claims = yes

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = GRP }
		release_targeted_tag_with_claims = yes

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = GOY }
		release_targeted_tag_with_claims = yes

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = RJM }
		release_targeted_tag_with_claims = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		occupy_medium_country = yes
		set_country_flag = BRA_CONQ
	}
}

				owns_state = 463
			}
			add_state_claim = 463
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = CAL
				owns_state = 473
			}
			add_state_claim = 473
			add_state_claim = 471
			add_state_claim = 740
			add_state_claim = 463
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = QUE
					state = 332 #Labrador
				}
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}

			QUE = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = QUE }
		puppet_released_tag = yes

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = CAN
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}

			CAN = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = CAN }
		puppet_released_tag_nocosmetic = yes
	}

	option = { #Liberate Quebec and annex Canada
		name = annex.188.e
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				tag = TEX
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = CSA
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = USA
				tag = CSA
				tag = TEX
			}
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = QUE
					state = 332 #Labrador
				}
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}

			QUE = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = QUE }
		puppet_released_tag = yes

		set_country_flag = CAN_CONQ
		occupy_small_country = yes
	}

	option = { #Annex Canada
		name = annex.188.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				tag = TEX
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				tag = CSA
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = USA
				tag = CSA
				tag = TEX
			}
		}

		set_country_flag = CAN_CONQ
		occupy_small_country = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = USA
				tag = CSA
				tag = TEX
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = RUS
				owns_state = 637
				owns_state = 463
			}
			add_state_claim = 463
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = CAL
				owns_state = 473
			}
			add_state_claim = 473
			add_state_claim = 471
			add_state_claim = 740
			add_state_claim = 463
		}
		occupy_large_country = yes
		set_country_flag = CAN_CONQ
	}

						}

			}
			SOM = {

		}

country_event = { #Annexation of Namibia
	id = annex.193
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.193" }
	title = annexation_NMB_CONQ
	desc = annexation_NMB_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			add_to_temp_array = { core_removal_array = PAR }
			remove_all_cores_and_claims_of_tags = yes
			NMB = {
				add_state_core = 541 #South West Africa
				add_state_core = 964 #Amboland
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.193.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = NMB }
		release_targeted_tag_with_claims = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { tag = GER }
				has_socialist_government = yes
			}
			NMB = { complete_national_focus = NMB_syndicalist_liberation }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { tag = GER }
				has_authoritarian_government = yes
			}
			NMB = { complete_national_focus = NMB_stern_state }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { tag = GER }
				has_elected_government = yes
			}
			NMB = { complete_national_focus = NMB_democratic_mandate }
		}
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = { is_ai = no }
		set_country_flag = NMB_CONQ
		occupy_medium_country = yes
	}
}

	desc = annexation_LIB_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes

		name = annex.210.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}

		trigger = {
			OR = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = authoritarian_democrat
				}
				tag = GER
				tag = MAF
			}
		}

		hidden_effect = {

				limit = {
					"LIB" = {

					set_party_name = {
						ideology = authoritarian_democrat
						long_name = "Deutscher Liberian Bund"
						name = "DLB"
					}
				}
			}
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = LIB }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
	}

	option = { #liberate authdem (anybody but Germany and Mittelafrika)
		name = annex.210.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}

		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = GER
				tag = MAF
			}
			has_government = authoritarian_democrat
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = LIB }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = authoritarian_democrat
				}
				"LIB" = {
					set_cosmetic_tag = LIB_AUTHDEM
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = authoritarian_democrat
						long_name = "Authoritarian Dem."
						name = "Authoritarian Dem."
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = LIB_CONQ
		occupy_small_country = yes
