country_event = { #Annexation of South Africa
	id = annex.219
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.219" }
	title = annexation_SAF_CONQ
	desc = annexation_SAF_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			SAF = {
				if = { #Clean up governor-general
					limit = {
						OR = {
							has_country_leader = { name = "Patrick Duncan" }
							has_country_leader = { name = "Nicolaas Jacobus de Wet" }
							has_country_leader = { name = "Ernest Janssen" }
							has_country_leader = { name = "George V" }
							has_country_leader = { name = "Edward VIII" }
							has_country_leader = { name = "Albert I" }
							has_country_leader = { name = "Henry IX" }
							has_country_leader = { name = "George VI" }
							has_country_leader = { name = "George Villiers" }
						}
					}
					kill_country_leader = yes
				}
				remove_ideas = SAF_wavering_dominion
				remove_ideas = SAF_neutral_dominion
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #liberate simple south africa
		name = annex.219.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = SAF
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
				NOT = {
					state = 542
					state = 545
				}
			}
			SAF = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = SAF }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
		SAF_puppet_setup = yes
	}

	option = { #with the protectorates
		name = annex.219.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_socialist_government = yes
					tag = MAF
					tag = GER
					tag = GEX
				}
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				owns_state = 542
				owns_state = 545
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = SAF }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		SAF_puppet_setup = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		set_country_flag = SAF_CONQ
		occupy_medium_country = yes
	}
}

		name = annex.224.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}

		CYP = {
			add_state_core = 183
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = CYP }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
	}

	option = { #Give it to the Turks
		name = annex.224.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 200
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_in_faction_with = TUR
				TUR = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
				is_in_faction_with = OTT
				OTT = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
			}
		}


		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_in_faction_with = TUR
					TUR = {
						is_subject_of = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			TUR = {
				transfer_state = 183
			}
			else = {
				OTT = {
					transfer_state = 183
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Give it to Greece
		name = annex.224.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_in_faction_with = GRE
				GRE = {
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
			}
		}

		GRE = {
			transfer_state = 183
		}
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		occupy_small_country = yes
		set_country_flag = CYP_CONQ
	}
}

country_event = { #Fate of Indonesia
	id = annex.225
	title = annexation_INS_CONQ
	desc = annexation_INS_CONQ_desc

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.225"
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { country_exists = DEI }
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = { is_core_of = DEI }
					remove_core_of = DEI
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { tag = JAP }
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_claimed_by = JAP
						is_indonesia = yes
						NOT = {
							state = 333 #North Borneo
							state = 828 #Sabah
						}
					}
					remove_claim_by = JAP
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #liberate
		name = annex.225.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_german_tag = yes
				has_subject = GEA
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = INS }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		INS = {
			hidden_effect = {
				set_cosmetic_tag = JAP_INDIES
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = { tag = JAP }
					}
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
						elections_allowed = no
					}
					set_political_party = {
						ideology = authoritarian_democrat
						popularity = 60
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Give it to HOL
		name = annex.225.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			is_ally_with = HOL
		}
		add_to_temp_array = { target_cores_to_release = INS }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = HOL }
		transfer_territory_from_core_regions = yes
	}

	option = { #Give it to GEA
		name = annex.225.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			is_german_tag = yes
			is_ally_with = GEA
		}
		add_to_temp_array = { target_cores_to_release = INS }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = GEA }
		transfer_territory_from_core_regions = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
		}
		occupy_medium_country = yes
		set_country_flag = INS_CONQ
	}
}

			}
		}

country_event = { #annexation of Uruguay

	id = annex.245
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.245" }
	title = annexation_URG_CONQ
	desc = annexation_URG_CONQ_desc
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #puppet

		name = annex.245.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 99
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = URG }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
                if = {
				limit = { has_socialist_government = yes }
				URG = {
					create_syndicalist_uruguayan_government = yes
					remove_all_ministers = yes
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_elected_government = yes }
				URG = {
					random_list = {
						50 = { create_rightist_democratic_uruguayan_government = yes }
						50 = { create_leftist_democratic_uruguayan_government = yes }
					}
					remove_all_ministers = yes
				}
			}
			else = {
				URG = {
					create_autocratic_uruguayan_government = yes
					remove_all_ministers = yes
				}
			}

	desc = annexation_KUR_CONQ_desc

	option = { #Puppet Kurdistan
		name = annex.248.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = TUR
				country_exists = KUR
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				OR = {
					is_ally_with = IRQ
					is_ally_with = TUR
					is_ally_with = OTT
					is_ally_with = PER
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				OR = {
					tag = IRQ
					tag = PER
				}
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = KUR }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
	}

	option = { #Give them to KUR
		name = annex.248.b
		trigger = {
			country_exists = KUR
			NOT = {
				tag = IRQ
				tag = TUR
				tag = PER
				is_ally_with = KUR
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 80
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					is_ally_with = IRQ
					is_ally_with = OTT
					is_ally_with = PER
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				OR = {
					tag = IRQ
					tag = PER
				}
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = { is_core_of = KUR }
			KUR = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #give to IRQ ally
		name = annex.248.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = IRQ
				tag = TUR
				tag = PER
			}
			IRQ = { ROOT_can_grant_land = yes }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					is_ally_with = TUR
					is_ally_with = OTT
					is_ally_with = PER
				}
				NOT = { is_ally_with = IRQ }
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = IRQ }
		add_to_temp_array = { target_cores_to_release = KUR }
		transfer_territory_from_core_regions_and_add_claims = yes
	}

	option = { #give to TUR ally
		name = annex.248.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = IRQ
				tag = TUR
				tag = PER
			}
			var:354.owner = {
				OR = {
					tag = TUR
					tag = OTT
				}
				ROOT_can_grant_land = yes
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					is_ally_with = IRQ
					is_ally_with = PER
				}
				NOT = {
					is_ally_with = TUR
					is_ally_with = OTT
				}
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = var:354.owner }
		add_to_temp_array = { target_cores_to_release = KUR }
		transfer_territory_from_core_regions_and_add_claims = yes
	}

	option = { #give to PER ally
		name = annex.248.e
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = IRQ
				tag = TUR
				tag = PER
			}
			PER = { ROOT_can_grant_land = yes }
			OR = {
				owns_state = 417 #Western Azerbaijan
				owns_state = 421 #Kurdistan
				PER = { owns_state = 417 } #Western Azerbaijan
				PER = { owns_state = 421 } #Kurdistan
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					is_ally_with = TUR
					is_ally_with = OTT
					is_ally_with = IRQ
				}
				NOT = { is_ally_with = PER }
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = PER }
		add_to_temp_array = { target_cores_to_release = KUR }
		transfer_territory_from_core_regions_and_add_claims = yes
	}

	option = { #split TUR/IRQ
		name = annex.248.f
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = IRQ
				tag = TUR
				tag = PER
			}
			OR = {
				owns_state = 350 #Smyrna
				owns_state = 352 #Bursa
				owns_state = 417 #Western Azerbaijan
			}
			OR = {
				owns_state = 421 #Kurdistan
				owns_state = 819 #Sulaymaniyah
			}
			var:354.owner = {
				OR = {
					tag = TUR
					tag = OTT
				}
				ROOT_can_grant_land = yes
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				is_ally_with = IRQ
				NOT = { is_ally_with = 354.owner }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				is_ally_with = 354.owner
				NOT = { is_ally_with = IRQ }
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = 354.owner }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 350 #Diyarbakir
					state = 352 #Van
					state = 417 #Western Azerbaijan
				}
			}
			transfer_state_and_add_claim = yes
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = IRQ }
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 421 #Kurdistan
					state = 819 #Sulaymaniyah
				}
			}
			transfer_state_and_add_claim = yes
		}
	}

	option = { #Integrate
		name = annex.17.h
		trigger = {
			OR = {

				tag = IRQ
				tag = PER
			}
		}

country_event = { # The fate of an unified central America
	id = annex.255
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.255" }
	title = annexation_CEN_CONQ
	desc = annexation_CEN_CONQ_desc

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Release a loyal unified central America
		name = annex.255.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = CEN_conquered_release
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = { #Coring
				limit = {
					NOT = { is_core_of = CEN }
					OR = {
						state = 311
						state = 1071
						is_core_of = GUA
						is_core_of = ELS
						is_core_of = HON
						is_core_of = NIC
						AND = {
							is_core_of = COS
							OR = {
								COS = {
									is_subject_of = ROOT
								}
								316 = {
									is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				add_core_of = CEN
			}

			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = CEN
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
				CEN = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = CEN }
			puppet_released_tag = yes
			CEN = {
				clr_country_flag = CEN_centro_released
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = {
							has_socialist_government = yes
						}
					}
					load_focus_tree = Centroamerica_focus #Loads the Commie tree
					set_country_flag = CEN_centro_released
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = {
							has_elected_government = yes
						}
					}
					load_focus_tree = CA_DEM_focus
					set_cosmetic_tag = CEN_CON
					set_party_name = {
						ideology = social_democrat
						name = CEN_social_democrat_liberal
						long_name = CEN_social_democrat_liberal
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = {
							has_authoritarian_government = yes
						}
					}
					set_cosmetic_tag = CEN_REP
					load_focus_tree = CA_military_focus
				}

				if = {
					limit = {
						HON = {
							exists = yes
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
					}
					annex_country = {
						target = HON
						transfer_troops = no
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						GUA = {
							exists = yes
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
					}
					annex_country = {
						target = GUA
						transfer_troops = no
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NIC = {
							exists = yes
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
					}
					annex_country = {
						target = NIC
						transfer_troops = no
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						ELS = {
							exists = yes
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
					}
					annex_country = {
						target = ELS
						transfer_troops = no
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						country_exists = COS
						OR = {
							COS = {
								is_subject_of = ROOT
							}
							owns_state = 316
						}
					}
					annex_country = {
						target = COS
						transfer_troops = no
					}
				}
			}
			CEN_setleaders = yes
		}
	}

	option = { # Release every nation separately
		name = annex.255.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = release_cen_seperate
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					owns_state = 316
					COS = {
						exists = no
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = COS }
				release_targeted_tag = yes
			}

			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = GUA }
			release_targeted_tag = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					GUA = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
					311 = {
						is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
						is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
					}
				}
				GUA = {
					transfer_state = 311
					add_state_claim = 311
				}
			}
			GUA_setleaders = yes

			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = NIC }
			release_targeted_tag = yes

			if = {
				limit = {
					1071 = {
						is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
					}
				}
				NIC = {
					transfer_state = 1071
					add_state_claim = 1071
				}
			}
			NIC_setleaders = yes

			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = HON }
			release_targeted_tag = yes
			HON_setleaders = yes

			set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = ELS }
			release_targeted_tag = yes
			ELS_setleaders = yes
		}
	}
	option = { # Keep it annexed
		name = annex.255.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_global_flag = centroamerica_formed
					has_global_flag = demcen_formed
					has_global_flag = milcen_formed
				}
			}
			occupy_medium_country = yes
			set_country_flag = CEN_CONQ
			set_country_flag = CEN_CONQ2
		}
		else = {
			hidden_effect = {
				set_variable = {
					to_pay = 0
				}
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = GUA_CONQ
					country_exists = GUA
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				to_pay = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = HON_CONQ
					country_exists = HON
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				to_pay = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = ELS_CONQ
					country_exists = ELS
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				to_pay = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = NIC_CONQ
					country_exists = NIC
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				to_pay = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = COS_CONQ
						COS = {
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
					}
					316 = {
						is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				to_pay = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					to_pay > 4
				}
			}
			occupy_large_country = yes
			set_country_flag = CEN_CONQ
			set_country_flag = CEN_CONQ2
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					to_pay > 2
				}
			}
			occupy_medium_country = yes
			set_country_flag = CEN_CONQ
			set_country_flag = CEN_CONQ2
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					to_pay > 0
				}
			}
			occupy_small_country = yes
			set_country_flag = CEN_CONQ
			set_country_flag = CEN_CONQ2
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Fate of Constantinople
	id = annex.265
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.265" }
	title = annexation_CONSTANTINOPLE_CONQ
	desc = annexation_CONSTANTINOPLE_CONQ_DESC

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #transfer TUR/OTT
		name = annex.265.a
		trigger = {
			var:340.owner = { #Bursa
				OR = {
					tag = OTT
					tag = TUR
				}
				ROOT_can_grant_land = yes
			}
			NOT = {
				tag = GRE
				tag = BUL
				tag = OTT
				tag = TUR
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 773 #Constantinople
					state = 341 #Adrianople
				}
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_claimed_by = var:340.owner }
				remove_claim_by = var:340.owner
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = var:340.owner } }
				add_core_of = var:340.owner
			}
			var:340.owner = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
	}
	option = { #transfer to GRE
		name = annex.265.b
		trigger = {
			GRE = { ROOT_can_grant_land = yes }
			NOT = {
				tag = GRE
				tag = BUL
				tag = OTT
				tag = TUR
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 773 #Constantinople
					state = 341 #Adrianople
				}
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						is_claimed_by = GRE
						is_core_of = GRE
					}
				}
				add_claim_by = GRE
			}
			GRE = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
	}
	option = { #transfer to BUL
		name = annex.265.c
		trigger = {
			BUL = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
			NOT = {
				tag = GRE
				tag = BUL
				tag = OTT
				tag = TUR
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 773 #Constantinople
					state = 341 #Adrianople
				}
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						is_claimed_by = BUL
						is_core_of = BUL
					}
				}
				add_claim_by = BUL
			}
			BUL = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
	}
	option = { #annex
		name = annex.17.h
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = OTT
				tag = TUR
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1000
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 773
					state = 341
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_claimed_by = ROOT }
				remove_claim_by = ROOT
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT } }
				add_core_of = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #annex
		name = annex.17.h

				tag = GRE
				tag = BUL
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1000
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				OR = {
					state = 773
					state = 341
				}
			}
			add_claim_by = ROOT
		}
	}
	option = { #occupation
		name = annex.occupation

	desc = annexation_SIB_CONQ_desc

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #puppet

		name = annex.269.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 99
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = JAP
				NOT = { country_exists = TRM }
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 408 #Vladivostok
						state = 409 #Khabarovsk
						state = 560 #Nikolayevsk
						state = 562 #Okhotsk
						state = 637 #Kamchatka
					}
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				}
				add_claim_by = JAP
			}
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_siberia = yes
					is_core_of = SIB
					AND = {
						is_owned_by = ROOT
						OR = {
							state = 582 #Orsk
							state = 573 #Zlatoust
							state = 581 #Northern Urals
						}
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						ROOT = { tag = JAP }
						OR = {
							state = 408 #Vladivostok
							state = 409 #Khabarovsk
							state = 560 #Nikolayevsk
							state = 562 #Okhotsk
							state = 637 #Kamchatka
						}
					}
				}
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			SIB = {
				add_state_core = PREV
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = SIB }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = annex.269.c #give it to Transamur
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_in_faction_with = TRM
				TRM = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 300
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_siberia = yes
					AND = {
						is_owned_by = ROOT
						OR = {
							state = 582 #Orsk
							state = 573 #Zlatoust
							state = 581 #Northern Urals
						}
					}
				}
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			TRM = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #occupy

		name = annex.269.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}

		occupy_large_country = yes

		set_country_flag = SIB_CONQ
	}

		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					CAF = { is_ally_with = ROOT }
					tag = GER
				}
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = SUR }

	}
	option = { #transfer to CAF
		name = annex.270.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = CAF
				tag = GYA
			}

				exists = yes
				is_ally_of_ROOT = yes
			}
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {

				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}

				limit = { is_claimed_by = CAF }
				remove_claim_by = CAF
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = CAF } }
				add_core_of = CAF
			}
			CAF = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
	}
	option = { #transfer to GYA

		}

				tag = CAF

				exists = yes
				is_ally_of_ROOT = yes
			}
		}

			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = GYA } }
				add_core_of = GYA
			}
			GYA = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
	}
	option = { #incorporate
		name = annex.270.f
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = CAF
				tag = GYA
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1000
		}
		occupy_small_country = yes

			limit = {
				is_core_of = SUR
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_claimed_by = ROOT }
				remove_claim_by = ROOT
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT } }
				add_core_of = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #occupy

			NOT = {
				tag = CAF
				tag = GYA
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {

		}

country_event = { #The Fate of Italy
	id = annex.280
	title = annexation_ITA_CONQ
	desc = annexation_ITA_CONQ_desc

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.280"
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = ITA_CONQ
			if = {
				limit = { tag = AUS }
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							state = 783 #Trentino
							state = 39 #Southern Tyrol
							state = 736 #Austrian Littoral
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { is_core_of = ITA }
						remove_core_of = ITA
						add_claim_by = ITA
					}
					if = {
						limit = { is_core_of = SRI }
						remove_core_of = SRI
						add_claim_by = SRI
					}
					if = {
						limit = { is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes }
						add_claim_by = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = annex.280.a #Release as Italy
		trigger = {
			has_socialist_government = no
			NOT = {
				tag = AUS
				has_government = authoritarian_democrat
				country_exists = ITA
				ITA = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
				SRI = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 95
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					SIC = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
					SRD = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
				}
			}

		}
		clr_country_flag = ITA_CONQ


		# restore initial cores if they were removed
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 159 #Lombardy
						state = 160 #Venice
						state = 759 #Friuli
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_claimed_by = ITA }
					remove_claim_by = ITA
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = ITA } }
					add_core_of = ITA
				}
			}
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_european_italy = yes
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			ITA = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_ai = yes
				is_subject_of = ROOT
				is_italian_tag = yes
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				every_unit_leader = { set_nationality = ITA }
				every_navy_leader = { set_nationality = ITA }
				transfer_navy = { target = ITA }
			}
			ITA = {
				annex_country = { target = PREV transfer_troops = yes }
			}
		}

		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = ITA modifier = KR_liberated_us }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = ITA }
		puppet_released_tag = yes

		hidden_effect = {
			ITA = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_government = national_populist
						NOT = { has_idea = ITA_republic_federation }
						NOT = { has_completed_focus = ITA_REP_destroy_austrian_influence }
					}
					add_ideas = ITA_republic_federation
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_government = national_populist
						NOT = { has_idea = ITA_republic_unitary }
						has_completed_focus = ITA_REP_destroy_austrian_influence
					}
					add_ideas = ITA_republic_unitary
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_government = national_populist
						has_idea = ITA_republic_unitary
						has_completed_focus = ITA_REP_centralized_power
					}
					remove_ideas = ITA_republic_unitary
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_government = national_populist }
						NOT = { has_idea = ITA_republic_federation }
						NOT = {
							has_completed_focus = ITA_REP_nationalist_question
							has_completed_focus = ITA_REP_stable_democracy
						}
					}
					add_ideas = ITA_republic_federation
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea = ITA_federation_transition }
					remove_ideas = ITA_federation_transition
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea = ITA_federation_secure }
					remove_ideas = ITA_federation_secure
				}
			}
		}
	}

country_event = { #Offering land in Italy in exchange for faction membership
	id = annex.281
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.281" }
	title = annex.281.t

	desc = {
		text = annex.281.d.allitaly
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = offering_italy
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = annex.281.d.centralitaly
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = offering_papacy
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = annex.281.d.piedmont
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = offering_piedmont
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = annex.281.a #We'll take the deal
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 3
				FROM = { can_form_italy = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				OR = {
					tag = PAP
					tag = SRD
				}
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = { is_in_faction = yes }
			hidden_effect = {
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						is_subject = no
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
						NOT = { tag = ROOT }
					}
					country_event = annex.284
				}
			}
			leave_faction = yes
		}

		separate_peace_all_wars = yes

		FROM = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					if = {
						limit = { ROOT = { has_country_flag = offering_italy } }
						is_european_italy = yes
					}
					if = {
						limit = { ROOT = { has_country_flag = offering_papacy } }
						OR = {
							state = 764 #Viterbo
							state = 1005 #Umbria
							state = 157 #Marche
							state = 161 #Romagna
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { ROOT = { has_country_flag = offering_piedmont } }
						OR = {
							state = 1003 #Aosta Valley
							state = 158 #Piedmont
							state = 838 #Liguria
							state = 762 #Nice
							state = 735 #Savoy
							state = 943 #Upper Savoy
						}
					}
					is_not_claim_or_core_of_PREV = yes
				}
				ROOT = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_faction_leader = yes }
				add_to_faction = ROOT
			}
			country_event = { id = annex.282 days = 1 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = annex.281.b #We refuse
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				is_in_faction = no
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				OR = {
					has_war = yes
					tag = SIC
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = annex.283 days = 1 }
		}
	}
}

			effect_tooltip = { add_to_faction = FROM }
		}
		FROM = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = offering_italy }
				clr_country_flag = offering_italy

			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = offering_papacy }
				clr_country_flag = offering_papacy
				ROOT = { clr_country_flag = PAP_STATES_CONQ }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = offering_piedmont }
				clr_country_flag = offering_piedmont
				ROOT = { clr_country_flag = PIEDMONT_CONQ }
			}
		}
	}
}

						NOT = { has_government = national_populist }
						NOT = { has_idea = ITA_republic_federation }
						NOT = {
							has_completed_focus = ITA_REP_nationalist_question
							has_completed_focus = ITA_REP_stable_democracy
						}
					}
					add_ideas = ITA_republic_federation
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea = ITA_federation_transition }
					remove_ideas = ITA_federation_transition
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea = ITA_federation_secure }
					remove_ideas = ITA_federation_secure
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = annex.280.m #Release as Italian Federation
		trigger = {
			has_socialist_government = no
			OR = {
				tag = AUS
				has_government = authoritarian_democrat
			}
			NOT = {
				country_exists = ITA
				ITA = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
				SRI = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
				is_italian_tag = yes
				AND = {
					tag = AUS
					country_exists = VNC
					VNC = {
						has_country_flag = VNC_accepted_austrian_help
						has_country_flag = VNC_republican_revolt

				}
			}

		}

				}
				if = {

				}

				is_ai = yes

			}

				every_unit_leader = { set_nationality = ITA }
				every_navy_leader = { set_nationality = ITA }

				annex_country = { target = PREV transfer_troops = yes }
			}
		}

		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = ITA modifier = KR_liberated_us }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = ITA }
		puppet_released_tag = yes

		hidden_effect = {
			ITA = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = authoritarian_democrat
					popularity = 0.2
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_idea = ITA_republic_federation }
					remove_ideas = ITA_republic_federation
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_idea = ITA_federation_transition }
						NOT = { has_completed_focus = ITA_REP_stable_institutions }
					}
					add_ideas = ITA_federation_transition
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_idea = ITA_federation_secure }
						has_completed_focus = ITA_REP_stable_institutions
					}
					add_ideas = ITA_federation_secure
				}
				if = {
					limit = {

					}
				}
				else_if = {

						NOT = { country_exists = VNC }
					}

						name = "Giuseppe Volpi"
						picture = "gfx/leaders/VNC/Portrait_VNC_Giuseppe_Volpi.png"
						expire = "1965.1.1"
						ideology = authoritarian_democrat_subtype
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_country_leader = { name = "Pietro Ferdinando I" ruling_only = yes }
						country_exists = TUS
					}
					kill_country_leader = yes
				}
			}
		}

				NOT = { has_country_flag = offered_papacy_@ROOT }
			}
			NOT = {
				ITA = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
				SRI = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
				SRD = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
				SIC = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
				PAP = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
			}

country_event = { #The Fate of Piedmont
	id = annex.291
	title = annexation_PIEDMONT_CONQ
	desc = annexation_PIEDMONT_CONQ_desc

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.291"
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = PIEDMONT_CONQ
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = annex.280.b #Release as SRI
		trigger = {
			has_socialist_government = yes
			NOT = {
				is_italian_tag = yes
				country_exists = SRI
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_italian_tag = no
				OR = {
					ITA = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
					SRI = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
				}
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = PIEDMONT_CONQ

		# restore initial cores if they were removed
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 1003 #Aosta Valley
						state = 158 #Piedmont
						state = 838 #Liguria
						state = 1004 #Emilia
						state = 161 #Romagna
						state = 162 #Tuscany
						state = 157 #Marches
						state = 1005 #Umbria
						state = 764 #Viterbo
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_claimed_by = SRI }
					remove_claim_by = SRI
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = SRI } }
					add_core_of = SRI
				}
			}
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 1003 #Aosta Valley
					state = 158 #Piedmont
					state = 838 #Liguria
					state = 1004 #Emilia
					state = 161 #Romagna
					state = 162 #Tuscany
					state = 157 #Marches
					state = 1005 #Umbria
					state = 764 #Viterbo
					state = 762 #Nice
					state = 735 #Savoy
					state = 943 #Upper Savoy
				}
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			SRI = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}

		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = SRI modifier = KR_liberated_us }
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = SRI }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = annex.291.a #Release as SRD
		trigger = {
			has_socialist_government = no
			NOT = {
				country_exists = SRD
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_italian_tag = no
				OR = {
					ITA = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
					SRI = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
				}
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = PIEDMONT_CONQ

		# restore initial cores if they were removed
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						state = 1002 #Sassari
						state = 114 #Cagliari
						state = 1003 #Aosta Valley
						state = 158 #Piedmont
						state = 838 #Liguria
						state = 762 #Nice
						state = 735 #Savoy
						state = 943 #Upper Savoy
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_claimed_by = SRD }
					remove_claim_by = SRD
				}
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = SRD } }
					add_core_of = SRD
				}
			}
		}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 1003 #Aosta Valley
					state = 158 #Piedmont
					state = 838 #Liguria
					state = 1002 #Sassari
					state = 114 #Cagliari
				}
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			SRD = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}

		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = SRD }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = SIC_confed }
			set_autonomy = {
				target = SRD
				autonomy_state = kr_federated_state
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				SRD = {
					owns_state = 158
					NOT = { has_cosmetic_tag = SRD_piedmont }
				}
			}
			SRD = { set_cosmetic_tag = SRD_piedmont }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				SRD = {
					NOT = { owns_state = 158 }
					has_cosmetic_tag = SRD_piedmont
				}
			}
			SRD = { drop_cosmetic_tag = yes }
		}

		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = SRD modifier = KR_liberated_us }
	}
	option = {
		name = annex.280.i #Offer to SRD
		trigger = {
			is_faction_leader = yes
			has_socialist_government = no
			838 = {
				is_owned_and_controlled_by = ROOT
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
			}
			SRD = {
				exists = yes
				is_subject = no
				NOT = { is_faction_leader = yes }
				controls_all_owned_states = yes
				has_socialist_government = no
				NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = offered_piedmont_@ROOT }
			}
			NOT = {
				ITA = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
				SRI = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
				SRD = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
				SIC = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		SRD = {
			set_country_flag = offered_piedmont_@ROOT
			set_country_flag = offering_piedmont
			country_event = annex.281
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = annex.280.c #Give to ITA allies
		trigger = {
			NOT = { tag = ITA }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = SIC_confed }
			ITA = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0.5
				SRD = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = PIEDMONT_CONQ

		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = ITA modifier = KR_returned_land }

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 1003 #Aosta Valley
					state = 158 #Piedmont
					state = 838 #Liguria
				}
			}
			ITA = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = annex.280.e #Give to SRI allies
		trigger = {
			NOT = { tag = SRI }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = SIC_confed }
			SRI = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		clr_country_flag = PIEDMONT_CONQ

		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = SRI modifier = KR_returned_land }

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 1003 #Aosta Valley
					state = 158 #Piedmont
					state = 838 #Liguria
				}
			}
			SRI = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = annex.280.f #Give to SIC allies
		trigger = {
			NOT = { tag = SIC }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = SIC_confed }
			SIC = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				SIC = { has_country_flag = SIC_empire }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				SRD = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
			}
		}
		clr_country_flag = PIEDMONT_CONQ

		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = SIC modifier = KR_returned_land }

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 1003 #Aosta Valley
					state = 158 #Piedmont
					state = 838 #Liguria
				}
			}
			SIC = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = annex.280.g #Give to SRD allies
		trigger = {
			NOT = { tag = SRD }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = SIC_confed }
			SRD = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
			NOT = {
				AND = {
					tag = SIC
					owns_state = 838
					NOT = { has_country_flag = SIC_empire }
					controls_all_owned_states = yes
					SRD = {
						exists = yes
						is_subject = no
						NOT = { has_war_with = ROOT }
						controls_all_owned_states = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 200
		}
		clr_country_flag = PIEDMONT_CONQ

		reverse_add_opinion_modifier = { target = SRD modifier = KR_returned_land }

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_not_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = yes
				OR = {
					state = 1003 #Aosta Valley
					state = 158 #Piedmont
					state = 838 #Liguria
					state = 762 #Nice
					state = 735 #Savoy
					state = 943 #Upper Savoy
				}
			}
			SRD = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = annex.280.h #Make a deal with SRD
		trigger = {

country_event = {
	id = annex.296
	title = annexation_AST_restoring_australasia
	desc = annexation_AST_restoring_australasia_desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_AST_crowd1

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.296"
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = AST
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
				remove_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = annex.296.a #The New Guard can restore order
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				OR = {
					has_government = social_democrat
					has_government = social_liberal
				}
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = AST
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
				}
			}
			AST = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		add_to_faction = AST
		AST = {
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = national_populist
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				set_capital = 985
				AST_enact_entente_trade = yes
				AST_remove_republic = yes
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_idea = AST_new_unrest
						}
					}
					add_ideas = AST_new_unrest
				}
				country_event = austral.248
				remove_all_ministers = yes
				add_ideas = {
					AST_William_JR_Scott_hog_npo
					AST_John_F_Dynon_for_npo
					AST_Hubert_L_Primrose_eco_npo
					AST_Thomas_Blamey_sec_npo
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = { has_unit_leader = 2100 }
					}
					clr_country_flag = Thomas_Blamey_dead
					create_field_marshal = {
						name = "Thomas Blamey"
						picture = "Portrait_AST_Thomas_Blamey.png"
						traits = {
							old_guard
							politically_connected
							war_hero
							organizer
							thorough_planner
						}
						skill = 4
						attack_skill = 4
						defense_skill = 3
						planning_skill = 3
						logistics_skill = 3
						id = 2100
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = annex.296.b #The Governor General will rule in our name
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				has_authoritarian_government = yes
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -100
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = AST
				is_owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
				}
			}
			AST = {
				transfer_state = PREV
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = AST }
		puppet_released_tag = yes
		AST = {
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				set_capital = 985
				AST_enact_entente_trade = yes
				AST_remove_republic = yes
				country_event = austral.248
				remove_all_ministers = yes
				add_ideas = {
					AST_William_M_Hughes_hog_ade
					AST_Vernon_AH_Sturdee_for_ade
					AST_James_Mitchell_eco_ade
					AST_Thomas_Blamey_sec_npo
				}
			}

				}

				create_field_marshal = {
					name = "Thomas Blamey"

			}
		}

			factor = 80
		}
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				SIC = {
					exists = yes
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
				}

					exists = yes
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
				}

	option = {
		name = annex.332.a #Give it to PAR
		trigger = {
			PAR = { ROOT_can_grant_land = yes }

					owns_state = 1027

				}
				owns_state = 688

			}
		}

			factor = 20

				remove_claim_by = PAR
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = PAR } }
				add_core_of = PAR
			}

		}

			}
		}

			factor = 20
			modifier = {

		}

				remove_claim_by = BOL
			}

				limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = BOL } }
				add_core_of = BOL
			}
			BOL = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = annex.333.b #Split it between PAR and BOL

			owns_state = 1027
			owns_state = 688
			PAR = { ROOT_can_grant_land = yes }

		}

			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				BOL = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
				PAR = { is_ally_of_ROOT = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 5
				BOL = { is_ally_of_ROOT = no }
				PAR = { is_ally_of_ROOT = no }
			}
		}
		688 = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_claimed_by = PAR }
				remove_claim_by = PAR
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { is_core_of = PAR } }

				}
			}
		}
		save_global_event_target_as = canal_zone_main_patron

		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #Return it to EGY
		name = annex.367.b
		trigger = {
			EGY = { ROOT_can_grant_land = yes }
		}

			factor = 20

				factor = 0
				OR = {

					tag = NFA

					tag = RUS
					has_authoritarian_government = yes
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_actual_major = yes
				has_socialist_government = no
			}
		}
		EGY = { transfer_state = 753 }
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #Return it to OTT

			}

		ai_chance = {

					tag = GBR
					tag = NFA
					tag = GER
					tag = RUS
					has_authoritarian_government = yes
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_actual_major = yes
				has_socialist_government = no
			}
		}
		EGY = { transfer_state = 753 }
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #Keep it
		name = annex.367.d
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		set_country_flag = SUEZ_CONQ
	}

		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					state = 981 #Najran
					state = 982 #Asir
				}
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
			}
			transfer_state_and_add_claim = yes
		}
	}

	option = { #Integrate
		name = annex.17.h
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = OTT
				is_arabian_tag = yes
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 1000
		}
		add_state_claim = 982
		if = {
			limit = { owns_state = 981 }
			if = {
				limit = { tag = OTT }
				hidden_effect = {
					var:678.owner = { transfer_state = 981 } #Rub al Khali
				}
			}
			else = {
				add_state_claim = 981
			}
		}
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = {
			is_ai = no
			is_arabian_tag = no
		}
		occupy_small_country = yes
		set_country_flag = ASIR_CONQ
	}
}

country_event = { #Fate of KUBAN
	id = annex.400
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event annex.400" }
	title = annexation_KUB_CONQ
	desc = annexation_KUB_CONQ_desc

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #puppet
		name = annex.400.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_russian_tag = yes
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { tag_to_release = KUB }
		release_targeted_tag = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				tag = GER
			}
			KUB = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = market_liberal
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					set_popularities = {
						totalist = 0
						radical_socialist = 0
						syndicalist = 0
						social_democrat = 0
						social_liberal = 0
						market_liberal = 60
						social_conservative = 0
						authoritarian_democrat = 40
						paternal_autocrat = 0
						national_populist = 0
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				tag = UKR
			}
			KUB = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = market_liberal
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				set_cosmetic_tag = KUB_ukraine
				hidden_effect = {
					set_popularities = {
						totalist = 0
						radical_socialist = 0
						syndicalist = 0
						social_democrat = 0
						social_liberal = 0
						market_liberal = 60
						social_conservative = 0
						authoritarian_democrat = 40
						paternal_autocrat = 0
						national_populist = 0
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				tag = RUS
			}
			KUB = {
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = social_conservative
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					set_popularities = {
						totalist = 0
						radical_socialist = 0
						syndicalist = 0
						social_democrat = 0
						social_liberal = 0
						market_liberal = 0
						social_conservative = 60
						authoritarian_democrat = 40
						paternal_autocrat = 0
						national_populist = 0
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Form Don-Kuban Union
		name = annex.168.e
		trigger = {
			tag = DKB
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = KUB
				}
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
			}
			add_core_of = ROOT
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = DKB_union
	}
	option = { #Form Don-Kuban Union not Kuban
		name = annex.168.e
		trigger = {
			DKB = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_core_of = KUB
				}
				NOT = { is_claimed_by = DKB }
				NOT = { is_core_of = DKB }
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
			}
			add_core_of = DKB
		}
		DKB = { set_cosmetic_tag = DKB_union }
	}
	option = { #Integrate
		name = annex.400.b
		trigger = {
			is_russian_tag = yes
			NOT = { tag = DKB }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = KUB
				is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_resistance = yes }
					set_temp_variable = { original_compliance = THIS.compliance }
					set_temp_variable = { original_resistance = THIS.resistance }
					cancel_resistance = yes
				}
				start_resistance = KUB
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_compliance }
					set_compliance = original_compliance
				}
				if = {
					limit = { has_variable = original_resistance }
					set_resistance = original_resistance
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_claim_or_core_of_ROOT = no }
				add_claim_by = ROOT
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -20
		add_to_array = { RUS_integration_array = KUB }
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = annex.168.c #Give to Russia
		ai_chance = {
			base = 80
		}
		trigger = {
			is_russian_tag = no
			var:219.owner = {
				is_russian_tag = yes
				is_ally_with = ROOT
			}
		}
		add_to_temp_array = { target_cores_to_release = KUB }
		add_to_array = { target_cores_to_release = KUB }
		hidden_effect = {
			random_other_country = {
				limit = {
					is_russian_tag = yes
					is_ally_with = ROOT
				}
				set_temp_variable = { ROOT.tag_to_release = THIS }
			}
		}
		transfer_territory_from_core_regions = yes
		recheck_annexations = yes
	}

	option = { #occupy
		name = annex.occupation
		trigger = {
			is_russian_tag = no
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		occupy_medium_country = yes
		set_country_flag = KUB_CONQ
	}
}
